< Review>

The service itself, however, was terrible. Seated at the bar for twenty minutes until I asked a waitress if the bartender was ever going to take my order. Kind of annoying, didn‚Äôt even get offered water. Seating could be managed better. Strong drinks good food, though.</Review>

<userid>105885459164753733504<//userid>< user_name>
annette b< /user_name>
<Time>1617160056074< /Time><rating>3< /rating>< Text>
The vibe is chill. Happy hour is a decent price. I would go back. Only complaint is they didn't have all of stuff on their menu. Literally everything I wanted to try was not something they were serving right now, or they were out of something. I would strongly suggest they let people know that certain things are either seasonal, brunch only items, or not currently available. Either don't promote something you don't have, create a smaller evening menu which you can actually provide, or let the customers know, what is actually available. <response>None< /response><Gmap_id>0x80dce7a8b229337d:0xf3a81a6c096506fb</Gmap_id><Rating>4<//Rating>< text>
I'll preface this by saying this was a to-go order

I really wanted to try this place considering all the hype it has. I got the Blaze and Classic ramen with a chicken karage bowl. Both ramens were okay. The broth was very rich and creamy and had good pork taste. They give you a choice of protein (chicken, pork or tofu); I picked pork. The pork was a thick piece, which I prefer, and had good flavor with some charcoal taste. The Blaze was definitely unique and their signature ramen. The medium spicy was perfect for me. I also added black garlic to the classic ramen which was amazing. I definitely recommend getting the black garlic it you are a garlic person.

My only problem was that the noodle was too soft for me. It seemed like they cooked the noodle a little too long before they put it in the container. This caused the noodle to clump together and they cooked even more. By the time I got to the noodle, it wasn't great. Maybe it would've been better if I ate there.

The karage bowl was just okay. I didn't love the creamy sauce they put on top and the chicken was basically similar to a lot of other karaage bowls.<//text>

Glad I stumbled upon Silverlake Ramen yesterday evening (7/10/20) during my stroll in the Spectrum Shopping Center. Their sign that showed a yummy bowl of ramen with the title ‚Äúbest ramen in town‚Äù caught my eye (and oddly enough sign I typically go straight to reviews first). So I stopped by the host station to check out their menu and I pretty much decided to stay after being greeted warmly by the two hostesses.

Food: I had an awesome waitress Sophia gave me great recommendations which I was able to confirm from the Yelp reviews. To start, I ordered the Pork Belly Bun and my‚Ä¶. DELICOUSNESS!!! You must try- and the price is very good for the quality. It gave me the ‚Äúmelt in your mouth‚Äù experience. Ugh, can‚Äôt wait to go back. Since I‚Äôm a spicy chicken ramen lover, ordered The Blaze with Chicken at spicy level medium. This definitely got the job done. The bowl was huge, the portion was filling, and the two pieces of chicken were large. You really get what you pay for. The spice level was perfect. They also have add-ons like corn.¬† I also was very pleased with the brand

Atmosphere: beautiful. Inside is chill and upscale and they have plenty of seating. Great spot if you want to eat alone and people watch with patio views (which was what I did) or the shade patio open pace or inside with shade and still enjoy views. Great for social distancing and everyone is wearing masks.

Customer service: FIVE STARZZZ. I was honestly blown away at how well I was treated. Everyone was super friendly, from the host and especially my waitress, Sophia. She had a great attitude and knew a lot about the menu. Her friendliness really brightened up my day. On top of that, the manager came by to ask how I like the the pork belly bun and authentically shared about how they prepared it and he was glad I liked it. I had an unusually long wait for my ramen to arrive. I was clearly an oversight and everyone was so apologetic. Even the CHEF Henry came to my table to apologize and make it right. I was blown away- he was so sincere and I really appreciated the stellar service. I look forward to coming back with my family and friends.

100% recommend this place- can‚Äôt wait to return! I hope y'all stay consistent with the quality & service!<//text>

<Review>I have seen many good reviews of this place, so we decided to try it on Sunday and was very disappointed. I Would not recommend this place based on our experience today.
Sunday lunch for 2 adults 1 child was $54.

Food here was alright, not great at all.
I had the chicken sopes plate, chicken was good but overall plate was alright nothing to say "it's delicious". Horchata was served in a nice clay glass too narrow though, so be prepared to ask for drink refill before getting your food.

Husband was never offered tortillas with his plate which usually are included and brought along. The Super michelada was very salty, he complained and was brought a second one but was still very salty and seemed like they forgot the shot of tequila it should've had.

For my 7 year old, I especifically ordered one chicken enchilada. But was brought a plate with beans, rice and 2 enchiladas filled with what seemed like a salad of lettuce, sour cream and cheese on top. We though that was from the kids menu so we didn't complain but we were charged $10.99. Plus $1.49 for his drink which was regular water (everywhere else we have been to water is free).  Their kids plates should be $7.99 including a drink.

Be careful with the salsa they have in a bottle it is super spicy.

Customer service: The restaurant was not super busy at all, They had 3 waitresses. our waitress, came by only to take our order and deliver our food. Never came by to ask how we were doing, if we needed something else. There were two other waitresses that we very busy with their own tables coming by and asking how things were, being very attentive with their customers but while making rounds they would skip our table. we had to call them over the 2 times we needed something because our waitress was hiding somewhere. After taking our request they would send our waitress over to deliver it.

Overall, food was alright, portions seem small for price=1 star
restaurant was clean and ambiance was fair=1 star
customer service is lacking.
prices need improvement.<//Review>< pics>

<Text>My wife and I visited Menlo Park one Sunday when we happened to be in the bay area (we live in the central valley, but if we could we would attend here!).  This is a church where a lot of good things are happening!  We attended both a contemporary and traditional service, and both were outstanding.  We went to the main church, but there are apparently a variety of options, depending upon your preference. Music was awesome.  This is a big church building, but strategically placed screens made it so everyone has a good view of what is going on. John Ortberg was preaching when we came, and you will have to search far and wide to find another who will compare with this speaker.  Ortberg is articulate and inspiring. Following the service he prayed for us and a number of other individuals that came forward after the service.  He is not only a gifted speaker but author of a number of best selling books.

There is a lot going on here with children's ministries for families with children.   People were friendly and accepting.  The director of small groups and a number of other ministries greeted us and spent quite a while talking with us, explaining the various ministries of the church.  If you are from the bay area you have the wonderful opportunity to grow in the influence of this wonderful church body.  If not, you will have to content yourself with watching their sermons online as I do.<//Text><UserId.>103080185899855158347< /UserId.><Gmap_id>0x808fa4afe7a4a775:0x1c8dc0166f5e0bb3< /Gmap_id>< pictures>

< text>
I've been here on and off for a number of years - mostly because it's close and there are very few archery stores around the Bay Area. My experience with their knowledge and abilities has been fairly good. Except for arrow repair where it has been hit and miss. My experience on average of interacting with the staff has generally been fairly poor. It depends on who you talk with. The owner (I think), Wayne is usually friendly and helpful, but most of my other experiences with other staff has been ok to very poor. They can be pretty indifferent and unfriendly in my experience.

I would come here more often if the average staff experience was more friendly. It's a nice shop otherwise.< /text>

< text>
I've been going to Archery Only since The Bowrack in Richmond closed a few years back.  I'm from Richmond so it's a matter of convenience, but Archery Only is the last man standing. Turned out that going to Archery Only was a great step forward for me.  I've been shooting a bow for sixty years now and I've made huge improvements in the last few years.  Wayne and Roger at Archery Only got me fixed up with a fairly inexpensive Hoyt camo bow, and got me going with the .166 real skinny arrows; and then later, a matching left handed Hoyt -- my idea, to shoot both ways.  Total great support from the staff at Archery Only, for whatever you want to do.  And I don't even go bowhunting.  So Archery Only is totally recommended for anything you want to do shooting bow and arrow.  Anything.< /text>

<pics>None<//pics><Date>1509207471015</Date>< Review>
I've been a customer of archery only for a couple decades and I've bought all of my compound bows there...and always will. I highly recommend AO for your first bow purchase. These compounds are very easy to pick up and shoot...but
1) they do require tuning and the expertise AO provides is valuable
2) Form is crucial in archery and AO will help get you started in the right direction

Consider this when reading bad reviews. I've been in the shop when folks bring in their bow they purchased from a online discounter and expect the guys in the shop to drop everything to help them on a bow they didn't sell...for free of course. Also consider that when dealing with your bow they have other folks trying to purchase stuff, etc...so being a small business they may not be able to devote all of their time to just your issue. With a little patience, they have always got me squared away and will to you too.< /Review>
